 the listing agent and your client has unilaterally secured a new Realtor a=
nd wants the condo price reduced significantly. He also says he is no longe=
r paying the mortgage beginning this month even though your client has been=
 living at the condo. Please let
 me know if you are free to speak today to discuss this issue. Carolyn <u><=
